<div class="timeline-cq-wrapper section" id="timeline">
<div class="timeline__wrapper">
    <div class="crux-container">
                    <div class="crux-label-style--regular">Working for and with You</div>
            <div class="crux-section-header--small">The consumer victories we've won together:</div>
        
        <div class="timeline__container">
            <button class="crux-icons crux-icons-caret-slider-left timeline__button timeline__button--left" aria-label="Previous"></button>
            <div class="timeline__items">
                                                                <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem ">
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>1964</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Surgeon General’s Landmark Report on Smoking</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">1964</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Surgeon General’s Landmark Report on Smoking</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>For a decade, CR conducted independent testing and research to highlight the dangers of cigarettes. The Surgeon General’s Advisory Committee on Smoking and Health used CR’s work to draft its landmark report.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem ">
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>1968</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>U.S. Government Mandates Seat Belts</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">1968</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>U.S. Government Mandates Seat Belts</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>CR tests showed two-thirds of seat belts failed basic safety and durability tests, leading CR to call for better belts and for federal standards that incorporated crash testing. The government later mandated them.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO%20Images%202018/Homepage/carseat%20rv" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>1981</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Setting New Standards for Child Safety Seats</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">1981</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Setting New Standards for Child Safety Seats</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>When CR first crash-tested car seats, 12 out of 15 were rated Not Acceptable. After CR published its findings, the government required manufacturers to certify that their seats would pass a similar test.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO%20Images%202018/Homepage/fruit" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>1999</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Exposing the Dangers of Pesticides</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">1999</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Exposing the Dangers of Pesticides</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>In a study of U.S. Department of Agriculture data, CR found pesticide levels in some fruits and vegetables were too high. Shortly after, one of the pesticides was banned for use on food crops commonly consumed by children.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem ">
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>2010</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Consumer Financial Protection Bureau Created</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">2010</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Consumer Financial Protection Bureau Created</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>CR helped to mobilize support in Congress to create the CFPB, an independent agency responsible for overseeing the financial industry with powers to police abusive practices and to enact new consumer protections.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO%20Images%202018/Homepage/baby-bottle" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>2013</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Bisphenol-A Banned in Baby Products</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">2013</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Bisphenol-A Banned in Baby Products</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>CR was one of the first groups to test food packaging for BPA. After working to pass bans in several states, the FDA finally announced a federal ban on BPA in baby bottles and sippy cups (2012) and infant formula packaging (2013).</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO%20Images%202018/Homepage/car%20rv" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>2014</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>A Win on Backup Cameras</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">2014</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>A Win on Backup Cameras</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>After years of CR’s advocating for standards to address the problem of blind zones behind cars and trucks, the Department of Transportation finally required backup cameras in all vehicles less than 10,000 pounds by 2018.&nbsp;</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO%20Images%202019/Misc/Romaine_145x145" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>2018</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Warning Consumers to Avoid Romaine Lettuce<br>
</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">2018</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Warning Consumers to Avoid Romaine Lettuce<br>
</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>In the wake of repeated E.coli outbreaks linked to romaine lettuce, CR came out ahead of public officials in recommending people avoid all romaine lettuce. CR’s position compelled regulators, including the CDC, to issue strong warnings to consumers.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO-Images-2020/Misc/CR-victory-timeline-tesla-0220" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>2018</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Steering Automakers Toward Making Safer Cars</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">2018</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Steering Automakers Toward Making Safer Cars</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>In response to CR’s removal of the Tesla Model 3’s recommended status due to braking distance, Tesla issued an OTA update—the first time a software update was used to change a car’s physical performance. The car earned back its recommended status.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

                                                                                                            <div class="timelineItem-cq-wrapper">
    
<div class="timelineItem image">
            <div class="timelineItem__img">
            <div style="width: 145px;">
                <img class="cld-responsive" style="width: 145px" data-src="//article.images.consumerreports.org/w_auto,dpr_auto,t_timeline,f_auto/prod/content/dam/CRO-Images-2020/Misc/CR-victory-timeline-privacy-0220-v2" alt=""/>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title-block">
        <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold"><span>2018</span></div>
        <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Advancing Laws to Protect Consumer Privacy</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="timelineItem__description-block">
        <div class="border"></div>
        <div class="content">
            <div class="timelineItem__date crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small--bold">2018</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__title crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>Advancing Laws to Protect Consumer Privacy</p>
</div>
            <div class="timelineItem__description crux-body-copy crux-body-copy--small"><p>The California Consumer Privacy Act provided key individual privacy rights, such as the right to stop the sale of personal info. CR fought efforts to weaken the legislation, mobilizing CR members to call on legislators to enact privacy protections.</p>
</div>
        </div>
        <div class="border"></div>

    function trackPageLink(linkName, linkLocation, linkReferrer, linkPrefix, prop72) {

        if (typeof s_gi == 'undefined' || s_account === 'undefined') {
            console.warn('s_gi or s_account is not defined');
            return;
        }

        var s = s_gi(s_account);
        var prop58 = s.prop58;
        prop72 || (prop72 = s.prop72);
        clearPropVars(s);
        var prop48 = linkName;
        if (linkPrefix != null) {
            if (linkPrefix == 'social') {
                trackEvent(s, 'event3');
                s.eVar5 = linkName;
            } else {
                prop48 = linkPrefix + '-' + prop48;
            }
        }

        if (linkLocation != null)
            prop48 = prop48 + '-' + linkLocation;
        if (linkReferrer != null)
            prop48 = prop48 + '^' + linkReferrer;
        prop48 = s.pageName + ' | ' + prop48;
        s.prop48 = s.eVar48 = prop48;

        s.linkTrackVars = 'prop48,eVar48';
        if(prop72 != null){
            s.prop72 = s.eVar72 = prop72;
        }
        if (s.prop72)
            s.linkTrackVars += ',prop72,eVar72';

        if (s.eVar5)
            s.linkTrackVars += ',eVar5';

        if (linkName == 'donate')
            trackEvent(s, 'event24');

        if (linkLocation == 'header' || linkLocation == 'subheader')
            trackEvent(s, 'event32');

        if (linkLocation == 'footer')
            trackEvent(s, 'event33');
        if (prop58) {
            s.prop58 = s.eVar58 = prop58;
            s.linkTrackVars += ',prop58,eVar58';
        }
        s.tl(this, 'o', linkName);
        s.events = '';
        clearPropVars(s);
    }

    function trackEvent(s, event) {
        if (s.linkTrackVars.indexOf('events') == -1)
            s.linkTrackVars += s.linkTrackVars.length > 0 ? ',events' : 'events';
        if (s.linkTrackEvents.indexOf(event) == -1)
            s.linkTrackEvents += s.linkTrackEvents.length > 0 ? ',' + event : event;
        if (s.events.indexOf(event) == -1)
            s.events = s.apl(s.events, event, ',');
    }

    function clearPropVars(s) {
        s.linkTrackEvent = '';
        s.linkTrackVars = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < 75; i++) {
            s['prop' + i] = '';
            s['eVar' + i] = '';
            if (i <= 5)
                s['hier' + i] = '';
        }
        // 'pageName','channel','products' preserved
        svarArr = ['events', 'campaign', 'purchaseID', 'state', 'zip', 'server', 'linkName'];
        for (var i = 0; i < svarArr.length; i++) {
            s[svarArr[i]] = '';
        }
    }


    //todo: redefined this method because global navigation does not expose this method
    function readCookie(inName)
    {
        var theNameWithEquals = inName + "=";
        var theCookieArray = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < theCookieArray.length; i++)
        {
            var c = theCookieArray[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(theNameWithEquals) == 0) return c.substring(theNameWithEquals.length, c.length);
        }
        return "";
    }

    function getCookieField(c_name, f_name) {
        var c_value = getCookie(c_name);
        if (c_value == "")
            return c_value;
        c_value = unescape(c_value);
        var fields = c_value.split("&");

        for (i = 0; i < fields.length; i++) {
            var field = fields[i].split("=");
            if (field.length == 2) {
                if (field[0] == f_name) {
                    return field[1];
                }
            }
        }
        return "";
    }


    function getCookie(c_name) {
        var i, x, y, z, a;
        var cookies = document.cookie.split(";");

        for (i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
            x = cookies[i].substr(0, cookies[i].indexOf("="));
            y = cookies[i].substr(cookies[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
            x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
            z = z + "--" + x + "--";

            if (x == c_name) {
                return decodeURI(y);
            }
        }
        return "";
    }


    function updateCompareEventToSC(products) {
        if (products != "") {
            var scvars = {
                'linkTrackVars': 'events,eVar6',
                'linkTrackEvents': 'event9',
                'eVar6': 'compare',
                'events': 'event9',
                'products': products
            };
            updateGenericEventToSC(scvars);
        }
    }

    function updateGenericEventToSC(scvars) {
        var s = s_gi("cuglobal");
        for (var key in scvars) {
            if (key != undefined && key != 'undefined') {
                s[key] = scvars[key];
            }
        }
        s.t();
    }


    function updateBuyingGuideEventsToSC(name) {
        var scvars = {
            "pageName": "CRO:HomePage" + ":" + name,
                            "prop1": "HomePage",
                                        "prop2": name,
            'channel': 'cro',
            'prop9': 'free'
        };
        s.prop16 = s.prop16 || 'visitor';
        updateGenericEventToSC(scvars);
    }
